				<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
						<p>                    Vision is the cornerstone of good design and at the core of fearless innovation. The all-new 2014 Impala is proof of that, combining superior materials with meticulously crafted technology. Its bold stance and sculpted lines combine form with function to please the eye and effectively command aerodynamics for a smooth, dynamic ride. The interior is transformed into an environment of sophistication and authenticity featuring premium materials thoroughly crafted with masterful technique resulting in superior finish in every detail. Engineered for excellence. Designed for drivers. The 2014 Chevrolet Impala is a stunning reinterpretation of the premium sedan.</p></div>

<div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			Assertive, athletic design</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>From its bold, confident stance to its sweeping roofline, the all-new 2014 Impala is artistically sculpted for lasting impressions. Its a striking departure from the status quo. The powerdome hood, wide chrome grille, projector-beam headlamps and available LED daytime running lamps project the bold new face of Chevrolet. The provocative silhouette, sculpted bodysides and a choice of 18-, 19- or 20-inch <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2014-impala_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_2" class="ln disclaimer_1">wheels<sup></sup></a>contribute further to its dramatic appearance and head-turning profile.<br>
<br>
<br>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</p></div>
		</div>
</div>
</div></div>
<div class="section grid_col1_c1"><div class="mds-area-pf1">
	<div class="pf1a_parsys parsys_c1"><div class="mm_c3 section"><div data-id="" class="mod modMm_3 mds-cmp-content05 ui_position_float_rel ui_layer_top">
			<div class="inner" style="width: 980px; top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: -125px;">
			  <img src="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Vehicles/Cars/2014%20Impala/Model%20Overview/01_images/2014-impala-model-overview-exterior-cnt-well-1-1280X637-05-1.jpg" alt="Form and Function of 2014 Impala sports sedan" width="1280" height="637" class="mm"/></div>


</div>
</div>
</div>
</div></div>
<div class="grid_col2_c1 section"><div class="mds-area-pf2">
	<div class="pf2a">
		<div class="parsys_c1 pf2a_parsys"><div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			Style with intention</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>The all-new 2014 Impala has the graceful lines worthy of its iconic  nameplate. The exterior is characterized by smooth, flowing contours  that are not only visually stunning but also impressively aerodynamic.  Honed in the wind tunnel, the artistically aerodynamic shape contributes  to a wonderfully quiet ride and greater fuel efficiency with an  estimated 31 MPG <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2014-impala_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_0" class="ln disclaimer_1">highway<sup></sup></a> with the 2.5L 4-cylinder <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2014-impala_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_3" class="ln disclaimer_1">engine<sup></sup></a> or an EPA-estimated 29 MPG highway with the available 3.6L V6 engine featuring Direction Injection and Variable Valve Timing.<br>
</p></div>
		</div>

	<div class="parsys_cnt_well_1 parsys_c1"><div class="section grid_col1_c1"><div class="mds-area-pf1">
	<div class="pf1a_parsys parsys_c1"><div class="parbase cnt_hl_c2 section"><div class="mod modCnt_hl_2 mds-cmp-content07 cnt_hl_2">
	<h2 class="hl_t ">
					Confident performance</h2>
			</div></div>
<div class="section mm_c1"><div class="mds-cmp-content05 mm_1 mod modMm_1" id="">
	<img src="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Vehicles/Cars/2014%20Impala/Model%20Overview/01_images/2014-impala-model-overview-performance-cnt-well-1-980x316-01.jpg" alt="Sports sedan 2014 Chevy Impala on the road" width="980" height="316" class="mm"/></div>
</div>
</div>
</div></div>
<div class="grid_col1plus2_c2 section"><div class="mds-area-pf3 flex">
	<div class="pf3a">
		<div class="parsys_c1 pn3a"><div class="mm_c3 section"><div data-id="" class="mod modMm_3 mds-cmp-content05 ui_position_float_rel ui_layer_top">
			<div class="inner" style="width: 415px; top: -50px; margin-bottom: -50px; margin-left: -39px;">
			  <img src="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Vehicles/Cars/2014%20Impala/Model%20Overview/01_images/2014-impala-model-overview-performance-cnt-well-1-414X491-02.png" alt="Sports sedan 2014 Chevy Impala Engine" width="414" height="491" class="mm"/></div>


</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
	<div class="pf3bc">
		<div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			In just 6.8 seconds</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>At the heart of Impala lies the acclaimed 3.6L V6 engine boasting 305 horsepower and 0-60 mph in just 6.8 seconds. Direct Injection injects fuel closer to the combustion chamber for an efficient, powerful burn. At partial or full throttle, youll feel the powerful response. Variable Valve Timing consistently boosts power by providing near-peak torque over a wider rpm range. The available engines refined power and finely tuned precision contribute to the confident and strong ride Impala is known for, while preserving impressive efficiencies such as an EPA-estimated 29 MPG highway.<br>
</p></div>
		</div>
<div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			Agile ride and handling</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>                    The stiff body structure and grounded stance allowed engineers to tune ride and handling precisely for an impressive connected to the road experience. The premium electric rack-and-pinion steering system delivers crisp, responsive handling and excellent on-center feel. A tight steering radius combined with an available variable-effort feature, which increases the level of power assistance during low-speed maneuvers, offers the driver impressive command over city streets and sharp turns. In the end it creates a smooth, effortless ride. </p></div>
		</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="grid_col1plus2_c2 section"><div class="mds-area-pf3 flex">
	<div class="pf3a">
		<div class="parsys_c1 pn3a"><div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			Connected to the road</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>                  The grounded stance exudes an air of confidence, while its refined exterior design and profile leave a lasting impression whether in motion or standing still. But this longer wheelbase and sculpted, stiff body structure are at the center of a more commanding driving experience. The 2014 Impala is for the assured driver ready to enjoy each turn, every hill and whatever the road may bring.     <br>
</p></div>
		</div>
</div>
</div>
	<div class="pf3bc">
		<div class="mm_c3 section"><div data-id="" class="mod modMm_3 mds-cmp-content05 ui_position_float_rel ui_layer_top">

			  <img src="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Vehicles/Cars/2014%20Impala/Model%20Overview/01_images/2014-impala-model-overview-performance-cnt-well-1-648X496-03.jpg" alt="Sports sedan 2014 Chevy Impala deck lid view" width="648" height="496" class="mm"/></div>

<div class="grid_col2_c1 section"><div class="mds-area-pf2">
	<div class="pf2a">
		<div class="parsys_c1 pf2a_parsys"><div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			Sophisticated</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>The Impala interior has been transformed into a carefully crafted, exquisitely detailed environment with the drivers comfort and peace of mind its focus. A dramatic and innovative reinterpretation of the classic Chevrolet dual-cockpit instrument panel flows seamlessly around the driver, while visual accents such as available soft ice-blue ambient lighting ignite the senses. And with thoughtful design along with ingenuity, the 2014 Impala is spacious and comfortable, offering ample room for five passengers.      New options for further driving comfort include heated and ventilated front seats, heated steering wheel with a power tilt/telescoping feature and 4-way adjustable front head restraints that allow the driver and front passenger to position them for a more comfortable fit.</p></div>
		</div>
</div>
</div>
	<div class="pf2b">
		<div class="parsys_c1 pf2b_parsys"><div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			Authentic</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>Each and every detail of the Impala interior was thoughtfully selected and expertly crafted to come together in an exceptional driving environment tailored to its driver. Beautiful available burnished woodgrain trim perfectly complements chrome accents throughout, while exquisite French stitching accentuates the premium textures of soft-touch and available premium sueded microfiber or leather-appointed surfaces. Available ventilated front seats and a heated steering wheel round out the environment for greater overall comfort for both the driver and passengers. Its more than an interior  its the pinnacle of taste and intrigue.<br>
</p></div>
		</div>
</div>
</div>
</div></div>

				</ul>
			<span class="next"></span></div>
		</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
	<div class="pf3c">
		<div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			Innovative</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>Interior designers thoughtfully considered every inch and every aspect of the all-new driver-centric Impala, keeping drivers needs at the forefront of their minds. Innovative storage options can be found intuitively throughout Impala that thoughtfully preserve spaciousness. Theres smart storage in the door panels and armrest, as well as umbrella storage in the front doors, and integrated cup holders and phone storage in the console.      Items can be kept in reach but out of sight with hidden storage space behind the available color touch-screen radio or stowed away within hidden under-floor storage in the trunk. Then theres the available Driver Memory Package, another thoughtful convenience that gives you two preset positions for the 8-way power driver seat, power-adjustable steering wheel and exterior mirrors. Recall your saved settings with the touch of a button. It even makes exiting easier by pulling the available power seat and steering column back and out of the way.</p></div>
		</div>
</div>
</div></div>
</div>

	<div class="parsys_cnt_well_1 parsys_c1"><div class="section grid_col1_c1"><div class="mds-area-pf1">
	<div class="pf1a_parsys parsys_c1"><div class="parbase cnt_hl_c2 section"><div class="mod modCnt_hl_2 mds-cmp-content07 cnt_hl_2">
	<h2 class="hl_t ">
					Intuitive technology</h2>
			</div></div>
<div class="nav_tablay_c1 section"><div class="mod modNav_tablay_1 mds-cmp-content13 nav_tablay_1 cmp-style ui-type-button ui-custom-button-colors">

					<div class="mod modCnt_btn_1 mds-cmp-content02 cnt_btn_1">
						<span></span>
		</div>
					
				   <div id="nav_tablay_item_c1_0_1" class="mds-area-pf1" style="height:575px">
							<div class="partab parsys_c1"><div class="grid_col2plus1_c2 section"><div class="mds-area-pf3 flex">
	<div class="pf3ab">
		<div class="parsys_c1 pf2a_parsys"><div class="mm_c3 section"><div data-id="" class="mod modMm_3 mds-cmp-content05 ui_position_float_rel ui_layer_behind">
			<div class="inner" style="width: 980px; top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px;">
			  <img src="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Vehicles/Cars/2014%20Impala/Model%20Overview/01_images/2014-impala-model-overview-technology-cnt-well-1-980x554-01.png" alt="2014 Chevy Impala MyLink Screen 1" width="980" height="554" class="mm"/></div>


</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
	<div class="pf3c">
		<div class="mm_c3 section"><div data-id="" class="mod modMm_3 mds-cmp-content05 ui_position_float_rel ui_layer_top">
			<div class="inner" style="width: 280px; top: 75px; margin-bottom: 75px; margin-left: -1px;">
			  <h3 class="pt"
				>
				Be Entertained</h3>
		<div class="tx">
				<p>Customize your driving experience by arranging the icons and features on your available 8-inch color touch-screen along with the Driver Information Center to showcase the information or options you want most. Impala features the largest color touch-screen yet on a Chevrolet vehicle along with hidden storage behind the screen with a USB <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2014-impala_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_6" class="ln disclaimer_1">port<sup></sup></a> to store your phone or items. In Valet Mode, it even locks to help keep valuable items safe and securely out of reach. Once your screen and Driver Information Center are customized to your preferences, youre ready to bring your favorite music and entertainment with you.&nbsp;                  The new available Chevrolet <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2014-impala_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_4" class="ln disclaimer_1">MyLink<sup></sup></a> works with your compatible smartphone and Bluetooth wireless <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2014-impala_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_5" class="ln disclaimer_1">technology<sup></sup></a> to stream music and entertainment through the <a href="http://www.pandora.com/" onclick="getOmnitureLinktrackingCode('http://www.pandora.com/');" target="_blank">Pandora Internet Radio</a> mobile <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2014-impala_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_7" class="ln disclaimer_1">app<sup></sup></a>.      Or you can listen to commercial-free programs through the 3-month trial of SiriusXM Satellite <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2014-impala_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_8" class="ln disclaimer_1">Radio<sup></sup></a>. The latest Chevrolet MyLink even allows you to store up to 60 favorites, including radio stations, contacts, destinations, music and other media.<br>
</p></div>
		</div>


</div>
</div>
</div>
</div></div>
</div>
</div>
					<div id="nav_tablay_item_c1_1" class="mds-area-pf1" style="height:575px">
							<div class="partab parsys_c1"><div class="grid_col2plus1_c2 section"><div class="mds-area-pf3 flex">
	<div class="pf3ab">
		<div class="parsys_c1 pf2a_parsys"><div class="mm_c3 section"><div data-id="" class="mod modMm_3 mds-cmp-content05 ui_position_float_rel ui_layer_behind">
			<div class="inner" style="width: 980px; top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px;">
			  <img src="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Vehicles/Cars/2014%20Impala/Model%20Overview/01_images/2014-impala-model-overview-technology-cnt-well-1-980x554-02.jpg" alt="2014 Chevy Impala MyLink Screen 2" width="980" height="554" class="mm"/></div>


</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
	<div class="pf3c">
		<div class="mm_c3 section"><div data-id="" class="mod modMm_3 mds-cmp-content05 ui_position_float_rel ui_layer_top">
			<div class="inner" style="width: 280px; top: 75px; margin-bottom: 75px; margin-left: 0px;">
			  <h3 class="pt"
				>
				Get connected</h3>
		<div class="tx">
				<p>The latest evolution of available Chevrolet <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2014-impala_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_4" class="ln disclaimer_1">MyLink<sup></sup></a> infotainment is here and premiering in the 2014 Impala. It features an all-new intuitive interface with the latest, easy-to-use technologies. Put simply: its cutting-edge technology simplified. Its highly customizable so you can personalize the system to your preferences, and capable of linking up to 10 devices. Stay connected to work, family and friends with your hands safely on the steering wheel using Bluetooth wireless <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2014-impala_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_5" class="ln disclaimer_1">technology<sup></sup></a>. Simply pair your compatible Bluetooth-enabled smartphone with MyLink and say what you want to do whether its making a call or streaming music. By pairing your device or connecting to MyLink through one of the three available USB <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2014-impala_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_6" class="ln disclaimer_1">ports<sup></sup></a>, you can have access to your entire contact list, personal playlists and select mobile apps. Your smartphone even charges while connected to a USB <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2014-impala_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_6" class="ln disclaimer_1">ports<sup></sup></a>. Its technology you can use.<br>
</p></div>
		</div>


</div>
</div>
</div>
</div></div>
</div>
</div>
					<div id="nav_tablay_item_c1_2_1" class="mds-area-pf1" style="height:575px">
							<div class="partab parsys_c1"><div class="grid_col2plus1_c2 section"><div class="mds-area-pf3 flex">
	<div class="pf3ab">
		<div class="parsys_c1 pf2a_parsys"><div class="mm_c3 section"><div data-id="" class="mod modMm_3 mds-cmp-content05 ui_position_float_rel ui_layer_behind">
			<div class="inner" style="width: 980px; top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px;">
			  <img src="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Vehicles/Cars/2014%20Impala/Model%20Overview/01_images/2014-impala-model-overview-technology-cnt-well-1-980x554-03.jpg" alt="2014 Chevy Impala MyLink Screen 3" width="980" height="554" class="mm"/></div>


</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
	<div class="pf3c">
		<div class="mm_c3 section"><div data-id="" class="mod modMm_3 mds-cmp-content05 ui_position_float_rel ui_layer_top">
			<div class="inner" style="width: 280px; top: 75px; margin-bottom: 75px; margin-left: 0px;">
			  <h3 class="pt"
				>
				Take control</h3>
		<div class="tx">
				<p>Impala offers the most intuitive, easy-to-use available Chevrolet <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2014-impala_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_4" class="ln disclaimer_1">MyLink<sup></sup></a> yet, with technologies that give you more innovative options for control. Make phone calls, select radio stations, choose music from your mobile device and more through natural language voice commands. There are no key phrases to remember and no need to look at a screen. This is innovation that makes connectivity a whole lot simpler. Its technology anyone can use. Steering wheel-mounted controls right at your fingertips give you immediate access to features in the Driver Information Center. Take navigation to the next level of ingenuity with on-screen OnStar Turn-by-Turn <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2014-impala_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_9" class="ln disclaimer_1">Navigation<sup></sup></a>, standard for six months. Receive directions through an on-screen display and hear directions from an automated voice. Destinations can also be spoken/saved as favorites. The available enhanced Chevrolet MyLink Radio with Navigation includes full navigation features as well as 2-D/3-D maps, points of interest, and SiriusXM <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2014-impala_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_9" class="ln disclaimer_1">NavTraffic<sup></sup></a> with a 3-month trial. Its all conveniently connected right to your Chevrolet MyLink system.<br>
</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p></div>
		</div>


</div>

	<div class="pf3a">
		<div class="parsys_c1 pf3a_parsys"><div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			<img src="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Vehicles/Cars/2014%20Impala/Model%20Overview/01_images/2014-impala-model-overview-technology-cnt-well-1-44X42-04.png" alt="" width="44" height="42" class="img"/><span>
						Voice and gesture recognition</span>
				</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>The latest available Chevrolet MyLink system offers natural-language voice recognition that allows you to place calls, enter destinations, browse media and play music with simple natural speech. Or you can accomplish various tasks using gestures, such as a swipe across the screen, similar to systems commonly used on mobile devices.<br>
</p></div>
		</div>
</div>
</div>
	<div class="pf3b">
		<div class="pf3b_parsys parsys_c1"><div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			<img src="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Vehicles/Cars/2014%20Impala/Model%20Overview/01_images/2014-impala-model-overview-technology-cnt-well-1-44X42-05.png" alt="" width="44" height="42" class="img"/><span>
						Keyless Access</span>
				</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>Theres no need to hunt for your key fob in your purse or pocket  with  this available feature, simply press the sensor on the door handle and  the door will unlock. And then as long as the key fob is inside the car,  you can start the engine with the push of a button.<br>
</p></div>
		</div>
</div>
</div>
	<div class="pf3c">
		<div class="pf3c_parsys parsys_c1"><div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			<img src="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Vehicles/Cars/2014%20Impala/Model%20Overview/01_images/2014-impala-model-overview-technology-cnt-well-1-44X42-06.png" alt="" width="44" height="42" class="img"/><span>
						Full-color touch-screen</span>
				</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>The 8-inch diagonal color touch-screen has a power up/down feature that  reveals a hidden behind-screen storage compartment with a USB <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2014-impala_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_6" class="ln disclaimer_1">port<sup></sup></a>,  so you can charge and store your phone while driving. You can even  customize the look of the on-screen graphics with one of four available  themes.<br>
</p></div>
		</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="grid_col3_c1 section"><div class="mds-area-pf3">
	<div class="pf3a">
		<div class="parsys_c1 pf3a_parsys"><div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			<img src="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Vehicles/Cars/2014%20Impala/Model%20Overview/01_images/2014-impala-model-overview-technology-cnt-well-1-44X42-07.png" alt="" width="44" height="42" class="img"/><span>
						Rear vision camera</span>
				</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>The available rear vision camera on Impala displays a rear view on the  touch-screen located conveniently in the center stack for easy view.  This feature helps you see stationary objects behind your Impala when  traveling in reverse at low speeds. The cross-traffic alert option also  alerts you to oncoming cross traffic while backing up.<br>
</p></div>
		</div>
</div>
</div>
	<div class="pf3b">
		<div class="pf3b_parsys parsys_c1"><div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			<img src="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Vehicles/Cars/2014%20Impala/Model%20Overview/01_images/2014-impala-model-overview-technology-cnt-well-1-108X42-08.png" alt="" width="108" height="42" class="img"/><span>
						Bose Surround Sound</span>
				</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>Everything in the all-new Impala, including the sound quality of your  music, is made for total driving enjoyment. The available 11-speaker  Bose Centerpoint Surround Sound System has been carefully tuned to the  interior acoustics of Impala.<br>
</p></div>
		</div>
</div>
</div>
	<div class="pf3c">
		<div class="pf3c_parsys parsys_c1"><div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			<img src="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Vehicles/Cars/2014%20Impala/Model%20Overview/01_images/2014-impala-model-overview-technology-cnt-well-1-44X42-09.png" alt="" width="44" height="42" class="img"/><span>
						USB ports</span>
				</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>Access music and entertainment stored on your phone while driving simply  by connecting your smartphone to the simple-to-use available Chevrolet  MyLink <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2014-impala_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_4" class="ln disclaimer_1">system<sup></sup></a> through three USB <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2014-impala_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_6" class="ln disclaimer_1">ports<sup></sup></a>.  With two ports in the console and another tucked away in the hidden  storage compartment behind the color touch-screen, you can charge  multiple devices while on the road.<br>
</p></div>

			</div></div>
<div class="section mm_c1"><div class="mds-cmp-content05 mm_1 mod modMm_1" id="">
	<img src="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Vehicles/Cars/2014%20Impala/Model%20Overview/01_images/2014-impala-model-overview-safety-cnt-well-1-980X316-01.jpg" alt="2014 Chevy Impala Sports Sedan in traffic" width="980" height="316" class="mm"/></div>
</div>
<div class="grid_col2plus1_c2 section"><div class="mds-area-pf3 flex">
	<div class="pf3ab">
		<div class="parsys_c1 pf2a_parsys"><div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			Preventive measures</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>Safety was a top priority when designing the all-new 2014 Impala. So Impala features some of the most innovative and ingenious advances in safety technology from standard StabiliTrak<sup> </sup>to available                 Crash Imminent Braking.</p>
<p>The Advanced Safety Package, available on LT and standard on LTZ, features additional available technologies and the optional Forward Collision Alert, which scans for vehicles ahead and alerts the driver to potential crash risks. Also available on LTZ, opt for additional safety features including Full-Speed-Range Adaptive Cruise <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2014-impala_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_10" class="ln disclaimer_1">Control<sup></sup></a> and enhanced Forward Collision Alert with                 Crash Imminent Braking, which utilizes radar in the front grille to sense traffic ahead. Adaptive Cruise Control adjusts or maintains vehicle speed accordingly when set to maintain follow distance. The enhanced Forward Collision Alert with&nbsp;                Crash Imminent Braking  can automatically apply the brakes to help avoid a front end collision or reduce impact speed.<br>
</p></div>
		</div>
<div class="section mm_c1"><div class="mds-cmp-content05 mm_1 mod modMm_1" id="">
	<img src="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Vehicles/Cars/2014%20Impala/Model%20Overview/01_images/2014-impala-model-overview-safety-cnt-well-1-648X316-03.jpg" alt="2014 Chevy Impala Sports Sedan traffic" width="648" height="316" class="mm"/></div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
	<div class="pf3c">
		<div class="section mm_c1"><div class="mds-cmp-content05 mm_1 mod modMm_1" id="">
	<img src="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Vehicles/Cars/2014%20Impala/Model%20Overview/01_images/2014-impala-model-overview-safety-cnt-well-1-316X177-02.jpg" alt="2014 Chevy Impala Sports Sedan side mirror" width="316" height="177" class="mm"/></div>
</div>
<div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			New assistance technologies</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>Impala is ingenuity put to work for the safety of you and your passengers, featuring newly available safety technologies that help give the driver not only &quot;eyes in the back of their head&quot; to aid in rear vision, but also help alert the driver to their sides and blind spots as well. Using radar sensors, Forward Collision Alert identifies vehicles ahead and alerts the driver to any potential crash risk while Rear Cross-Traffic Alert alerts the driver to crossing traffic from behind while the vehicle is in reverse. Similar radar sensors keep an eye on blind spots to the side of the vehicle with the Side Blind Zone <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2014-impala_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_11" class="ln disclaimer_1">Alert<sup></sup></a>, which illuminates small LED-lit symbols in the corresponding outside mirror when another vehicle is detected. Impala even keeps an eye on your driving with the available Lane Departure Warning. It gives you an audible alert while driving if you unintentionally drift out of your lane without using a turn signal.<br>
</p></div>
		</div>
</div>
</div></div>
</div>
</div></div>
<div class="grid_col1plus2_c2 section"><div class="mds-area-pf3 flex">
	<div class="pf3a">
		<div class="parsys_c1 pn3a"><div class="section mm_c1"><div class="mds-cmp-content05 mm_1 mod modMm_1" id="">
	<img src="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Vehicles/Cars/2014%20Impala/Model%20Overview/01_images/2014-impala-model-overview-safety-cnt-well-1-316X247-04.jpg" alt="" width="316" height="247" class="mm"/></div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
	<div class="pf3bc">
		<div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			Protection and response</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>In the event of a collision, the vehicles innovative safety features go to work helping to protect with 10 standard <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2014-impala_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_1" class="ln disclaimer_1">air bags<sup></sup></a>. Structural integrity of the vehicle is important during a collision and Impala provides a strong, stiff body using ultra-high-strength steel. Theres also the safety and support of <a href="#content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2014-impala_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_12" class="ln disclaimer_1">OnStar<sup></sup></a>, standard for six months, with Automatic Crash Response. In many crashes, built-in sensors can automatically alert an OnStar Advisor, who is immediately connected to your Impala to see if you need help. Even if you dont respond, an OnStar Advisor can use GPS technology to pinpoint your exact location and request that emergency help be sent right away.</p></div>
		</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>

	<h2 class="hl_t ">
					HOW SUSTAINABLE IS THE IMPALA?</h2>
			<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
						<p>Check out its Ecologic features. Here at Chevrolet, we believe in being a responsible steward of our environment. Weve developed a way to communicate some of the environmentally significant features of each vehicle we make. We call it Ecologic.<br>
</p></div>
				</div></div>
<div class="mm_c3 section"><div data-id="" class="mod modMm_3 mds-cmp-content05">
			<div class="inner">
	<img src="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Shared%20Resources/01_images/2014-chevrolet-model-overview-ecologic-cnt-well-1-308x76-01.jpg" alt="" width="308" height="76" class="mm"/></div>

<div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>Every aspect of Ecologic is audited by Two Tomorrows, an independent third-party sustainability auditor. To learn more about Ecologic and the Two Tomorrows process, click here. <br>
</p></div>
		</div>
</div>

	<div class="pf3bc">
		<div class="section mm_c1"><div class="mds-cmp-content05 mm_1 mod modMm_1" id="">
	<img src="/content/dam/Chevrolet/northamerica/usa/nscwebsite/en/Home/Shared%20Resources/01_images/2014-chevrolet-model-overview-ecologic-cnt-well-1-648x315-02.jpg" alt="" width="648" height="315" class="mm"/></div>

<div class="grid_col2_c1 section"><div class="mds-area-pf2">
	<div class="pf2a">
		<div class="parsys_c1 pf2a_parsys"><div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			Fuel-Saving Technologies</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>Continuously Variable Valve Timing (VVT) adjusts airflow in and out of the combustion chamber under all engine speeds, which helps improve fuel economy and lower emissions.</p>
<p></p>
<p>With Direct Injection, fuel is injected directly into the combustion chamber, which allows for a higher compression ratio and results in better fuel economy.</p>
<p></p>
<p>Electric Power Steering uses an electric motor instead of an engine-driven belt, resulting in a lighter overall workload and better fuel economy.<br>
</p></div>
		</div>
</div>
</div>
	<div class="pf2b">
		<div class="parsys_c1 pf2b_parsys"><div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			Responsible Manufacturing</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>  The transmission facilities are landfill-free. These facilities use a process to reuse, recycle or convert to energy all waste created in their daily operations, which conserves resources.</p></div>
		</div>
<div class="modCnt_par_1 mod cnt_par_1 section mds-cmp-content01"><h3  class="pt">
			End-of-Life Recyclability</h3>
		<div class="fck_authorsinput tx">
				<p>  After the vehicles useful life, 85% of it is recyclable. The majority of its components can be broken down and recycled, which conserves resources and reduces landfill deposits.</p></div>
		</div>
</div>
</div>

						<li id="content_chevrolet_northamerica_usa_nscwebsite_en_index_cars_2014-impala_model-overview_jcr-content_cnt_legalpage_c1_disclaimers_disclaimer_c1_0">

								Estimate based on GM testing.</li>
